		<div class="grid-header-box">
			
			<h2 class="grid-title"><a href="https://gas2.org/2018/03/06/formula-e-season-5-nissan-reveals-2018-19-race-car/">Formula E Season 5:  Nissan Reveals 2018-19 Race Car</a></h2>

							<div class="grid-post-box-meta">
											<span class="author-italic">by <a href="https://gas2.org/author/joborras/">Jo Borrás</a></span>
																<span>March 6, 2018</span>
									</div>
					</div>

					<div class="item-content">
				<p>Formula E Season 5 is coming for 2018-19, and the sport has a new race car and new manufacturer support- highlighted today as Nissan Revealed its 2018-19 livery!</p>
